in motocayotiah aztecacalpoltin oquimocahuilitoh inhuehuetlaltzin itocayocan aztlan auh niman ic omopanolticoh hueyi colhuacan
izcatqui iniqueon calpoltin intocatzin  matlatzincah  tecpanecah  chichimecah  malinalcah  cuitlahuacah  xochimilcah  chalcah  huexotzincah
quinyacanayah nahuixtin pipiltin in calpoltin intocatzin catca tezcacoatl cuauhcoatl apanecatl auh zatlatzaccan chimalma
tezcacoatl quimamaya huitzilopochtli
oquizque hueyi colhuacan ihuan itzintla hueyicuahuitl in cuauhmayo catca mocehuicoh ompa momoztli conquetzacoh noihuan otlacuacoh auh quilmach huitzilopochtli tenahuati ma yehuantin moxexeloah quihto
cecni ma huian chiconcalpoltin ihuan oc cecni ma nehnemican nohuan in mexicah
mochintin huecauhtica chocacticatcah auh niman omoxexeloque
mexicah opanocque guextecatlichocayan ihuan oacicoh coatlicamac nozo coatepec ipan ome calli xihuitl
coatepec omochiuh xiuhtlalpilli ipan ome acatl xihuitl ihuan mexicah oquilhuiquixticoh zanyeno oncan inic ce yancuic intleuh in oyuh oquizque in ihuicpa aztlan
cempoalchiconxiuhtique coatepec ihuan omotlalicoh tollantzinco ipan ei tecpatl xihuitl
mihtoa in mexicah tepalehuicoh inic pololoz hueyi imaltepeuh in toltecah
ye cempoalxihuitl in ohuecauhque tollantzinco oyaque mexicah atlitlalacyan in canin oacicoh ipan mahtlactli tecpatl xihuitl
yehuan omotlalique atlitlalacyan mahtlactli xihuitl
ipan chicueyi acatl xihuitl oacicoh tlemaco in canin zan macuilxiuhtique
zatepan omicuanique atotonilco in canin oacicoh ipan mahtlactli omeitecpatl xihuitl ihuan zanyeno oncan nauhxiuhtique
atotonilco quicauhque ipan yei acatl xihuitl ihuan omotlalique apazco ipan nahui tecpatl xihuitl
oquilhuiquixtique apazco inic ome yancuic intleuh ipan orne acatl xihuitl in oyuh ocaxiltique occe imaxca xiuhmolpilli
ipan yei tecpatl xihuitl omicuanicoh tzompanco in oncan nauhxiuhtique
oquizque mexicah in ihuicpa tzompanco ipan chicuace acatl xihuitl auh ic niman ipan chicome tecpatl xihuitl oacique yehuan in xaltocan in canin ohuecauhque nahui xihuitl
omotlalitoh acalhuacan ipan mahtlactli once tecpatl xihuitl ihuan zanyeno oncan onenque ixquichca ce acatl xihuitl
niman omicuanique ehecatepec in mexicah ipan ome tecpatl xihuitl ompa nauhxiuhtique in yehuantin
ipan chicuace tecpatl xihuitl oyaque tolpetlac in oncan omotlalique ixquichca mahtlactli omei acatl xihuitl
ce tecpatl xiuhpan omotlalicoh coatitlan in mexitin
inoyuhcempoalxiuhtique coatitlan mexicah oyaque chalco canatoh metl oc quiyeyecoah coatitlan in octli in ayamo hui yehuantin huixachtitlan
chicueyi tecpatl in xiuhpan omicuaniah mexitin huixachtitlan in oncan zan nauhxiuhtiah
ipan mahtlactli omome tecpatl xihuitl oyaque mexicah tecpayocan
ihcuac oacic ome acatl xihuitl yaoyotl oncatca ompa omomiquilitzinoque tecpatzin huitzilihuitzin ihuan tetepantzin
noyuhqui mexitin ocaxiltique occe xiuhtlalpilli tecpayocan ihuan oncan quilhuiquixtique inic ei yancuic intleuh
ipan yei tecpatl xihuitl mochiuh inic ce immotlaliliz pantitlan in oncan noihuan ohuetz cocoliztli innacayo mexicah tzatzayanticatca
ic niman ipan chicome tecpatl xihuitl oacique mexitin amalinalpan in tlein itech pohui azcapotzalco itlahtocayotzin
azcapotzalco itlahtocatzin tezozomoctli catca
amalinalpan chicuexiuhtique in mexicah
omocuepque niman in pantitlan ipan ome tecpatl xihuitl in canin ocaxilticoh nahui xihuitl
ipan chicuace tecpatl xihuitl omicuanicoh acolnahuac in oncan nauhxiuhticoh
niman ic ipan mahtlactli tecpatl xihuitl omotlalicoh popotlan in oncan ohuecauhque nahui xihuitl
ipan ce tecpatl xihuitl omotlalique mexicah techcatitlan in canin onenque ixquichca nahui acatl xihuitl
in ye ce xihuitl in oacicoh techcatitlan omotlahtocatlali tenoch
ohuiah niman in mexitin motlalitoh atlacuihuayan yehuatl on omochiuh ipan macuilli tecpatl xihuitl
yehuantin quitocayotique atlacuihuayan ihuan inin altepepan quinextique atlatl ihuan mitl atlacuihuayan zan nauhxiuhtique
zatlatzonco ipan chiconahui tecpatl xihuitl omotlalicoh mexicah chapoltepec ohuecauhque mexicah chapoltepec cempoalli xihuitl
ocaxiltique chapoltepec ipan ome acatl occe imaxca xiuhmolpilli yeceh ahuel yehuantin quilhuiquixtiah yancuic intleuh ye ipampa yaoyotl oncatca
tecpanecah ihuan colhuacah oquimpeuhque mexicah in aquique quichoquilique inin impopololiz huitzilihuitl ihuan icihuapiltzin azcalxochitl quinhuicaque in oquic tlalpiltin catcah ixpan cocoxtli itlahtocauh colhuacan
ipan yei tecpatl xihuitl cocoxtli oquincauh mexicah mamotlaliah tizapan inic in cocoah quimmictizque auh in mexicah oquincuacque ihuan aocmo oncatca in cocoah tizapan itech pohuia contitlan
ihcuac onenque contitlan quintlacachiuhque in mexicah miectin inconehuan
ipan chicuacen acatl xihuitl cocoxtli colhuacan itlahtocauh oquinchihuili yaoyotl xochimilcah
ic niman oquinyaonotzqui mexicah quinec quimpehuaz in xochimilcah intepalehuiliztica mexitin
quimilhui xiquintequilitih ce innacaz xochimilcah in amehuan ma xiquimilpiecan niman xinechhualhuiquiliquih nacaztli xiquipilco
yehuan oquimanque miequintin xochimilcah yeceh amo quintequilique innacaz zan ye quincotonilique inyac inic amo momatiz in tlahtoani ca zan tlahco quimilpique
omauhcatzatzic cocoxtli in oyuh quittac pexonqui xixiquipilli
ca iniqueyin mexicah amo tlacah zan tecuanime
ihcuac omocauh in mitl in chimalli teocalli conquetzque ihuan quitlatlauhtilique cocoxtli ma huallauh tetlamaniliz tlahtoani quintitlan iixiptlahuan in oquimanilique cuitlatl cualancayotica mexicah quimmictiah iixiptlahuan in cocoxtli ihuan mochintin colhuacah in monexitiah
ipan chicome tecpatl xihuitl quitzintique mexicah altepetl in motocayotia mexicaltzinco yehuatl in inahuac iztapalapan oc axan moquetza

quintepan ipan mahtlactli omome xihuitl mochantilicoh iztacalco yeceh ompa zan yei xihuitl onenque
niman zoquipan inchantzinco in oncan oacicoh ipan ce acatl xihuitl

ohuiah noyuhqui mexicah omaltitoh in temazcalco
ipan ce tecpatl xihuitl quimottahtocatlalitzinoque acamapichtzin yuh inic ce hueyi intlahtocatzin
ye cexihuitl in omotlahtocatlali acamapichtli otzintic hueyi altepetl mexico tenochtitlan
mihtoa in ihcuac oacique mexicah in tlalhuacton in tlein icpac hueyi atezcatl oncatca acatlan oquittacoh ce cuauhtli in aquin tenochpan icaya ihuan quicuaya in coatl

in quexquichcauh maniz in cemanahuatl aic ixpolihuiz in inteyo in itauhca in mexicotenochtitlan

ipan chicueyi tecpatl xihuitl omotlahtocatlali huitzilihuitl in aquin oteyacan mexico cempoalli once xihuitl huitzilihuitl nepapan tlacah oquimpeuh iteyacancayopan yuhquin toltitlan cuauhtitlan chalco tollantzinco xaltocan otompan tetzcoco ihuan acolman
ocaxiltique mexicah occe imaxca xiuhtlalpilli ic yehuan oquilhuiquixtique inic ce yancuic intleuh tenochtitlan zanyeno ihcuac temocque in chapolme ihuan in millan cualocque
huitzilihuitzin omomiquilitzino ipan ome tecpatl xihuitl
ipan yei calli xihuitl quitlahtocatlalique tenochcah in chimalpopoca inic ei hueyi tlahtoani mexico iteyacancayopan chimalpopoca mochiuh omaltepetlalique in chalcah iniqueyin oquimmomotlacque tenochcah in huallayah ipan nahui acalli ihuan oquimmictique macuilli yehuantin chimalpopoca oquinyaochiuh tihuetz chalcah ihuan occepa quimpopolo

tollan aya huapalcalli manca nozan in mahmani coatlaquetzalli ya quiyacatehuac nacxitl topiltzin     on quiquiztica ye choquililo in topilhuan     ahuay ye yauh in polihuitiuh nachcan tlapallan ho ay

nonohualco ye nihuitz ye nihui quecholi nimamalitecutla nicnotlamatia     oyahquin noteuc ye ihuitimali nechyaicnocauh nimatlacxochitl ayao ayao o ayya yyao ay
in tepetl huitomica niyaichoca ya axalihqueuhca yehua yan nicnotlamatia oyahquin noteuc

panquetzaliztli niman ye atemoztli tititl izcalli atlacahuallo in ipan onmotlatocatlalli in cuauhtemoctzin tlacaxipehualiztli in quimonpeuh in chalca ihuan xocotitlan tlaca niman quitaque tehuan mohuahuanque tzotzontli ipan in micque pipiltin tzihuacpopoca xoxouhpehualloc tzihuactzin tencuecuenotl axayaca totlehuicol
inic mic tzihuacpopoca quinahuati in cuauhtemoc amantlantlenamaca quimilhui in tiachcahuan ye omilhuitl in notlan hualcecemilhuitia in tzihuacpopoca ma itlan nechaiti
niman quitoa in tiachcahuan maca quimoyolli tlacalhui in tlacatl tlacoculizcuitiz ma tiachcahuan ma yauh   niman ye monahuatia in tlamacazque no yehuantin in tiach cahuan in temictizque niman ye quitetemohua in oquittaque mohuehuetzquilitihui in cuauhtemoctzin niman ye iquech tlancanato quilhuia   oc xihualla on niccauhtze
niman ye quihuihuitetequi hueytotoztli niman ye toxcatl etzalcualiztli ipan intech cempohualtique in cristianome tecuilihuitontli hueytecuilhuitl niman ya miccailhuitontli   ic napohual tonatiuh in ica xihuac mexicayotl tenuchcayotl
ic 10° totlatohuani ochpaniliztli in onmotlatocatlali cuitlahuatzin zan napohualilhuitl tlatocat quecholli tlami in ipan mic totomonaliztli in ic omic ihcuac yaque in tlaxcalla caxtillan tlaca
ic 11° in tlatohuani ipan motlatocatlalli cuauhtemoctzin ihuan oncan moyahuac in mexicayotl tenuchcayotl ihcuac hualcencalacque in españoles
zan tlaocolxochitl tlaocolcuicatl on mania mexico nican ha in tlatilolco in yece ye oncan on neiximachoyanohuay
ixamayo yectli in zanca otitechicneli ipalnemohuani in za can tipopolihuizque in timacehualta ohuaya
ototlahueliltic zan titolinia timacehualtin      que zo huel tehuantin otiquittaque in cococ ya machoyan
ticmomoyahua ticxoxocoyan in momacehual in tlatilolco cococ moteca cococ ye machoyan ye ic ticiahuia      ic ye titlatzihuia ipalnemohuani ohuaya
choquiztli moteca ixayo pixahui oncan in tlatilolco in atlan yaque o in mexica ye cihua nelihuia ica huiloa can on tihui in tocnihuan ohuaya
inic nel ticoyacahua atloyantepetl o in mexico in poctli ehuatoc ayahuitl in mantoc      in ah ihcuac in tlepan quixtilico in coyohuacan ohuaya
in anmexica ma xicilnamiquican o ya zantopan quitemohuia iellel imahuizo  anqui ya oncan in coyonacazco
za can ye oncan zan quinchoquiztlapaloa      o anqui huizmanatl in zan ye i motelchiuh onya aquin ye mochin ha in tlailotlaquia in tlacotzin ah in tlacatecutli in oquihtzin ihuihui ica zan ya conyacauhqui in tenochtitlan ohuaya
o in antocnihuan ma xa chocacan aya      ma xocon matican ica ticcauhque mexicayotl huiya      zan ye atl chichix huia no zan ye tlacualli chichix aya zan con ayachiuhqui in ipalnemohuani ha in tlatilolco
tel ah zan ihuian huicoque on      in motelchiuhtzin ha in tlacotzin     zan mocuicaellacuahuaque acachinanco      in ah ihcuac in tlepan quixtilico in coyohuacan ohuaya
nihualacic yenican ye niyoyontzin huiya zan nicxochi elehuia yeehuaya in xochintlan tlapanacoyan tlalticpac ye nican nocoyatlapana in cacahuaxochitl nocoyatlapana icniuhxochitl ye tehua monacayo titetepiltzin nezahualcoyotl teuctli yohyontzin yyao ohuili yya ayyo yao aya ahouiya
zan ye nitemohuitihuitz mocuic in yectli ihuan nicyatemohuan tictonihuan aya     ma onpapacohua yehua icniuhtlamachoyan
achin ic nonahuia o achin ye ompahpactinemi noyollo in tlalticpacqui ye niyoyontzin nixochiehelehuia oo nixochincuicuicatinemi ohuaya
nicnehnequi nicehelehuia in icniuhyotl in tecpillotl nixochiehelehuia oo nixochincuicuicatinemi ohuaya
o anca yuhquin chalchihuitl ohuaya      zanca ca yuhquin cozcatl in quetzallinpatlahuac ipan ye nicmati yectli ye mocuica ya  ica nonahuia ica nonitoti ya huehuetitlan o xopancalitic i ye niyohyontzin noyollo quimatiohuaya
ma xicya huelin tzotzona moxochihuehueu ticuicanitl yeehuaya ma izquixochitl man cacahuaxochitl      ma on moyahua ya ma on tzetzelihui ye nican huehuetitlan ma  tahuican i ohuaya ohuaya
ya zanca xiuhquechol tzinitzcan tlauhquechol oncan oncuicantlatohua ya in xochitl ic paqui
a oncan icaqui i xochincuahuitl i huehuetitlan ayahue zan ye itech onnemi in quetzalinquechol in tototl ipan mochiuhtinemi o nezahualcoyotzin on xochicuicuicatinemi in xochitl ic paqui
cuauhyotica oceloyotica ma onnequechnahualo antepilhuan     icahuanca in chimalli  cohua malimanico y yao ayyaha      zan topan moyahua ya topan tzetzelihuia necalizxochitl in ahualtiloca in ipalnemoani 
in pozoniyan ye oncan zan miliniyan in tlachinolliyan mahuizzotiloyan nechimaltocayotiloyan    oyohualpan teuhtlamotecayan ohuaya ohuaya
o ahqueman on tlatzihuiz yaoxochitl mani yeehuaya atoyatempan in oncuepontimanique oceloxochitl in chimallixochitl i     oyohualpan teuhtlamotecayan ohuaya ohuaya
a oceloncacahuaxochitla ya onca ya mani ya zanca i tzetzeliuh in ixtlahuatl itic i      zan topan ahuiazticaco o conanquinequi o anca ye timallotl in mahuizotl ohuaya
o ahcemelle xochitl ahcemelle ahuia mochiuhticac i yolloxochitl ixtlahuacan yaonahuac oncan quiza ya in tepilhuan o anca ye timallotl in mahuizotl ohuaya
in cuauhtehuehueltica ocelopanitl i nepanihui yeehuaya quetzallinchimaltica ye onnemamanalo zacuanpanitl huitolihui onpozonia ye oncan ohualehua ya in chalcatl o amaqueme o ayohuilo ihcahuaca yaoyotl ohuaya ohuaya
in tlacotl xaxamantoc itztli teintimani o chimalteuhtli topan ya moteca ya 
nihuinti nichoca nicnotlamati nicmati nicitoa nicelnamiqui      maca aic nimiqui maca aic nipolihui
incan ahmicohua incan ontepetihua in ma oncan niauh      maca aic nimiqui maca aic nipolihui
nichoca yehua nicnotlamati             zan nicelnamiqui ticcauhtehuazque yectli ya xochitl yectli ya cuicatl                in ma oc tonahuican ma oc toncuicacan cen tiyahui tipolihui yehua oahuaya
ach tle on ayuhquimati in tocnihuan i cocoya noyollo cualani yeehuaya ayoppan tlacatihua ayoppan piltihua             i yece ye quixhuan tlalticpac ohuaya
ma oc achitzinca i tetloc yenican tenahuac ayahue aic yez aic nahuiaz aic nihuelamatiz ohuaya
in canon nemian noyollo yeehuaya             ca huel ye nochan ca huel nocal amaniz  ninotolinian tlalticpac ohuaya
timotolinia noyolo yeehuaya              ma xicnentlamati tlalticpac yenican             o anca yuhqui notonal ahuaye quimati ohuaye huixahue canon nicmacehuia in mach yuhcan nitlacat in tlalticpac ixama ihuiya ehuaya ic yectli ya huelihui ahcampa nemoa zan quitoa noyol a ohuaya
quen quitoa aya nellon tinemi              aya nellon tiyahuecahuaco tlalticpac
o aya nicyacahuaz yectli ya xochitl      aya nicyatemohuiz quenonamican huiya      o anca cihui zan achic zan tictotlanehuia yectl on cuicatl ohuaya ohuaya
nepapan cuauhtli omitoque oncan texcalco in mochantxa in motapazoltia in tlatlazo in tlatlapana auh inic quimana ipilhua tompiatli anozo o tla chiquihuitl miicac quiquetza in anqui in ihcuac cualani in cuauhtli quimotzolotehua in tompiatli quihuica huel huecapan in quihuica ompa quihuallaza in momati azo yez yeh in tlamani in oquihualcauh niman huallalatzacatiten o ipan hueca quimonaxitia in ipilhuan nacatl in itlacual cuauhtli
huactli mocozcacuahnenehqui inic tlatoa in quenmanian yuhquin ma haca tlacatl huehuetzca yuhquin ma tlacatlatoa huel quitenquixtia inic tlatolli yeccan yeccan yeccan inic huetzca quitoa hahahahaha hahay hahay hahay hahay occenca ihcuac in quitta in itlacual huel huehuetzca
auh inic huillotl itoca ca itech tlaantli in itlatol in quitoa huilo auh inic huillotl quil quilhuique in occequintin totome    ma tihuia tatatacazque tatlizque
quil cenca motachcauh nequia ihuan cenca tlatzihuia zan huetztoc in quihualnotza quimilhuia   ma huilohua   amo nel ye huiloa
auh in oquinextique atl ic mochi tlacatl quimaceuh in ihuian atlihuaz in yocoxca atlihuaz auh in tlamacazqui ca nel nozo amo otehuan atatacac quil oncan conmocahuilli amo tehuan atliz ic zan yohualtica in quiixtacatatl auh motocayoti yahui itoca mochiuh in yehuatl tlamacazqui in huillotl ipampa zan quitoaya ma huilohua
auh inic maci in ozomatin  huey tletl motlalia cintli moyahualochtia anozo tlaolli auh in tleco quimotoca cenca huey in cacalotetl auh in tlamani in anqui motlaltoca
auh in ye popoca in manel cahui cate in yehuantin ozomatin quihualinecui in tletl in poctli niman hualhui quimmamama in impilhuan cololhuiti moteca in tletl pehua in mozcohua pehua in mocinizquia in mocalhuia mocuecuepa in mozcohua quincuecuepa in impilhuan in quimozcoa in quintotoma
auh moicucic cacalotetl canel nozo aquittaz in tletl niman cueponi huel tlatzcueponi xittocueponi huel ihui in    tlequiquiztli in nextli moyahua cen mani in tlexochtli impa cen mani yehuantin ozomati in nextli in ixco calaqui ic motlaloa choloa yuhquin aca quintoca quintlatztehua quimmamayauhtehua in impilhuan manel nozo oc quitemoa aocmo quimitta

auh ayac oc ce tlacatl canatiuh in ompa icac i no elaquiloc huel conomatcahuiaya in tlamacazque teopixque quil amo teuhque amo tlazolloque ipanpa inin omaconana
auh inic moztlacahuiaya quitohuaya inin oelaquiloc ompa oya in ilhuicac in tocayocan tlalocan ompa quititilani in teteu tlaloque ic cenca quimahuiztiliaya inic conana in imic quitlapechtica in quihuica quitocazque in ayauhcalco quitlapiechililihui quitolcaltia
auh intla aca tlapalihui canaznequiz in oelaquiloc in amo zo aca teuhyo tlazollo quil no ompa quihualanazque amoce ompa quiahui huey cocoliztli in itoca cohuacihuiztli
auh inin elaquilo quil cualli in iyollo ipanpa in ompa quihuica tlalocan auh anoce quipia chalchihuitl quil ic cualani in tlaloque ca quil nozo in nacayo manoce in itonal in chalchihuitl ipanpa in elaquilo tel quil no ompa yauh in tlalocan onpa titlano ic occeppa in papaquiliz catca itahua yolque quitoaya ca otlacnopilhui in ipiltzin ca onpa oya in tlalocan auh in yehuantin quil mocuiltonozque quil quimacehua in tonacayotl in huactli in chien etc
auh oc izca inic motlapololtiaya quil mach intla oc elaquiloc oc no yuhqui impan mochihuaz in oc cequintin in ihuayolque azo no elaquilozque anozo in ipan tlatlatziniz inic no ompa yazque in ilhuicac in itocayocan tlalocan
auh inin tlahuelilocayo in amo cenca matiaya yoyolito in ihcuac ayac imac huetzi in ayac quelaquia niman quihualpantlaza in mimichtin in xoxohuiltin in ahuilome in cuecueya tlapatlaca tlacocholihui in cuecueya onelnelcequi tlalhuacpan in no tlatlamotlatinemi mimichtin in iztac michtin no yuhqui quilihua in tlilcoatl 
auh in aqui matoahua yuhquim miicoltia quimitta mimichtin niman ye ic tlatlama quimocuicuixantia in mimichtin inin ca zan i tetlacaanaya in yolcalpil niman ye ic ipan pozoni in atl ic onca miqui oncan elaquilooncan popolihui oncan i poctla yauhtlan mochihua in popohuiztli in atlanonotzalli

in aquin za quitta in amo tle ipan quichihua in amo quelaquia quimotetzahuia quil miquiz amo quitetzahuia in yuhca nenonotzalli zan ipanpa cenca momauhtia in ca achi quil pitza ic miqui
ca ce tlacatl ilamaton quicuitihuetz ihuipil ic quitlapaeho niman apilolco contlaz atl contecac in ixpan quihuica in tlatoque huel quittaque anel nozo quimteuhmatia in yolcapil quil mach tlaloc quil tlamacazque  niman tlanahuatique occeppa onpa quicahuato in inpa canac ilamatzin quil miquiz in ilamatzin ca otlatlaco zan oquito
auh ihuan in coyotl tlatlazocamatini mocnelilmatini quin izqui quin ye topan ce tlacatl ipan quizato zacatla ecatico in coyotl utli quitocatiuh in tiacauh auh in coyotl niman ye quihualmanotza auh huel tlamahuizo ihuan huel motetzahui huel quimotetzahui in tiacauh
za ihuic yatia auh in oitechacito quittac cohuatl in itech omotetecuix iquechtlan quiztoc in cohuatl huel ic omotetecuix in itoca cincoatl auh iitic quito in tiacauh ac yeh in nitlaoculiz i
niman concuito in tiacauh in tlacotl in tetlacotl in ollacotl niman ye ic quihuihuitequi in coyotl ca aquittoz in tlacotl in cohuatl niman hualchapatihuetz in cohuatl ni   man ye yayatica in coyotl auh omozcali niman ye motlaloa azo omehoyatica in nepa milpan acito
in coyotl in tiacauh in oquimamaquixtili on tenco in totolme huexolome in quihuica in iixpan quimontlacato quitentopechtinemi ach yuhquima quilhuiznequi xiccui

auh inic quimana inic maci yehuatl in tecutlazauhqui in tlacotl in tetlacotl in ollacotl ic mohuitequi auh in zan iciuhca ic maci yahuatl in picietl in aquin canaznequi ic momatiloa in picietl niman no ic quimotla oc cenca intla icamac calaqui picietl in yehuatl coatl
niman zo tlahuatimoteca aocmo molinia ic za imatica conana mochiuhque in ixquichtin cocohua huel ic zotlamiqui in picietl

in ixochio i tecotlacozauhqui cohuacihuizpatli in canin onoc cohuacihuiztli oncan onmalahua in ixochic in iyehuayo atonahuizpatli coniz in atonauhqui
ca yuh omochiuh in ipan ce tlacatl in cecni teopixcalco quintequipanoaya in ompa teopixque ca itlacauh ixolouh intetequipanocauh catca ca nel inic tlatequipanoani tlacatl ca oquichtec cenca miec tomin in itech ompohuia in teopixcacalli auh in ye oquitech ca ceccan ixtlahuacan oquitlatocato oquitlapachoto inic zatepan quitatacaz quiquixtiz ihuan ic cholotehuaz
auh in ye choloznequi ca ohuia in canin oquitlaltocac in tomin inic quiquixtiz ihuan ic yatihuetziz auh izca ca in ye oncan onacito ca oquittac in ce huel huey temamauhti coatl in oquichololti in ichtecatlacatl
in occe tonalli ocnoceppa in oncan ohualla in ichtequi ihuan ocnocuelceppa oquittac in tecuancoatl in amo oquicauh in quiquixtiz in tomin ca zan ye coatl oquitepotztocac ihuan quinequia quimictiz intlacamo in ichtequi omotlaloani inic momaquixtiz
ocnocuelceppa ohualla in ichtequi inic quitlaltatacaz in tomin ihuan ocnocuelyexpa oquinamic in coatl auh yehuatlin coatl amo zan ye iyo oquitotocac in ichtequi ca ocnohuian in coatl oquitlaxili in icpoyo in iihiyo in ichtequi ic tlalpan ohuetz yuhquima ye omic
cequintin tlaca oquittaque ihuan cecni cocoxcacalco oquihuicaque inic quipatizque tel ahuel opatic in ixquich cahuitli in icochpan oquihualmottiti in cocoxqui ce huehue ya tlacatzintli in oquimahuili in ichtequi ihuan oquimolhuili ca niman aic patiz intlacamo quitecuipiliz in teaxca in tomin in oquichtec
ohualizac in ichtequi zanniman oquinotz in cocoxcapixqui ihuan oquipohuili in ichtequiliz ihuan in occequi in ipan omochiuh in cocoxcapixqui oquimmonahuatili in teopixque ihuan itencopa cequintin tlaca oquimomamaltique ihuan oquihuicaque in ichtequi in ompa in canin oquitlati in tomin
auh ye aocmo in oncan catca in tecuancoatl ic oquitlaltataque ihuan oquiquixtique in tomin in oichtecoc ihuan oquimmomatiquilique in teopixque imaxca catca ihuan zanniman ic opatic in cocoxcaichtequi
ica cualancayotl oquenin monequiz ocalaquito xochicalco ihcuac ompa ocalaquito nelli oquimicahuatzque topiltin quimilhuia   tlen mach amaxtaya ahuel anhualaya zazan anhuecahuato nican ye niapiazmiqui huan amehuantin amo annecia   tlen ipampa amo yehuatl huehue ancualicaque huan amo inin ixcuicuitla ancualicaque que inin amo nechpachihuitiz 
quitoa topiltin   amo oticualicaque huehue amo oquican hualaz nin pilalactli ipanpa on amo oticualicaque   quitoa xochicalcatl   amo nicnequi ocachi nicaquiz xinech huicxitlican ye niapiazmiqui
onahuaten tepoztecatl quilhuia in xochicalcatl   xinechcaqui huey tlacatl amo xicualani nian amo xiquimahua amo nicnequi tiquimicahuatzas topiltin yehuan amo quipia tlatlacolli nehuatl xinechchihuili tlen ticnequiz   oncan onahuaten xochicalcatl quilhuia tepoztecatl
amo xinechnananquili zan xitlamatza ixcuicuitla ximocuani xia xinechtlacolhui   imanon ocanteque topiltin nelli oquitlacalque itic huey caxitl canin huicciz nelli ahue ohuiccia nelli omocuepaya tequihua cuati michi huan nepa ye apizmiqui xochicalcatl
quinnonotzato non tlacualchique inic cuicazque nacatl huan nican amo quitami tlen quichihuazque oquineque nozo amo quinahuatito xochicalcatl huel nelli inaca ahuel huicci zan ompa oquimicahuatz oquintotocac quimilhuia   xiquizacan ame oncan amechtuahuiz xictlacaliti itic tlalcomitl ompa man huicciti
nelli ocuicaque quitlacalito itic tlalcomitl nelli ompa occeppa ye tlemach mocuecuepa nelli mocuepa mazatl totli tochtli coyotl tecuani ocelotl opeque occeppa tlatequipanoque ye momotia ahuelli huicci in piltontli huan xochicalcatl ye cualani yecapizmiqui
icuac oquimittac occeppa ye oquizatotlanahuatito non tlacualchique cahuel ahuelli huicci non piltontli zan tlemach yolcame mocuepa nelli quimilhuia   tle quimach anquizaco nican quimach amo totopetihuitze tlen iyolcayo anechhualliquilique ahuelli huicci huan nehuatl ye niyecapizmiqui 
quitoa topiltin    tehuan amo ticmati tehuan oticualicaque piltontli huan amo yolcatl    otlahualnahuat xochicalcatl quimilhuia    xinechanilitin zazo quenin yez nicuaz inic ye niapizmiqui
itzitzicuinteque inintin canato tepoztecatl oquicalaquique itlac xochicalcatl nelli niman quilhuiti   hueyi tlacatl nican tinechpia mixpan tlenon ticnequi xochicalcatl nahuati quilhuia    nicnequi tinechilhuiz aquinon tehuatl piltontli
nahuati tepoztecatl huan quitoa    nehuatl nitepoztecatl nialtepecaconetl mocuitia tepoztlan nehuatl onihualla niquinmaquixtico mochtin altepeme ya oticmat tlen notoca huan canin nochan axcan tlen ticnequi mochicahua noyolo   xochicalcatl tlanahuati  xictzacua mocamac ayecmo nicnequi nicmatiz ocachi ximocamatzacua tlen tichchihuaz ximoyolpepena nia timitzcuaz
occeppa nahuati tepoztecatl nelli quitoa tepoztecatl  tinechcuaz man timitzilhui tla tinechcuaz nozo amo tinechtetequiz tla melac zan tinechtoloz zanque nimoquetztica nian amo tinechtlanteciz zan no centeixti tinechtoloz
nelli oquito xochicalcatl  ma xihuelihui ye niapizmiqui   melac nelli tlen oquichin tepoztecatl nelli omotocti imahuan huan nelli quilhuia  axcan xicamazohui huan ompa nia  melac nelli ocamazon xochicalcatl huan nelli tzentzicuintin in tepoztecal opanotiquis icenteixti icamac zan oquitolo
huan itahuan tepoztecatl otlachixtiaya non cozcatlan o mate cozcatzinco oquichixtaya mehuaz poctli que oquimilhuiten oncan nelli xochicalcatl iman ya huecapa ontlatolo open camacoyahui tzatzi momimiloa motlalhuihuitequi tzitzicuini nepa ca nican moteca itetenehui itecualo opeque tlatlani tlen cocoliztli quipiaya teuctli ihcuac oquimatque ye miqui tlacayehui opeque tlatla occequintin tlamelac ya miquiznequi ihcuac oquimatque melec ya omic
nelli zan oitetonehuia huan nelli imanon tepoztecatl open tlatequi itic xochicalcatl ocuitlaxcoltetec ica itztli huan tecpatl oquinechicota iman ocuicaque huan iman oquitolo zan ica nochi amo manel oquitlatemolique
tel zan ica inon omic iman ye omic xochicalcatl tlen oquichin tepoztecatl oquiitetzomoni xochicalcatl huan oquiz tepoztecatl melac omic xochicalcatl melac nelli omacoc poctli chipahuac quename ce ichcatl iman oquitaque poctliicolhuan tepoztecatl omacoc tlahuelchipahuac nelli omolhui que
axcan quema ye otlatlan toconen amo miqui ne mi man ticchiate tochan ya calaquin   nelli melac inime oyaque ichan ye quichiato tepoztecatl ye otlatlan
oyeya cente puchtecatl oquipiaya yeyi ipilhuan zuantonton cosa cuacualtzitzin nochipa cuac oyaya tlanamacatin oquintlatlaniaya tlenon oquinequia quinahualiquiliz nochipa oquihtlaniliaya cecente itlaquen cucualtzitzin   cecpa inon oc achi tzitziquitzin yocmo oquinec hualquiliz itlaquen zan oquitlanili cente xochitl niman puchtecatl oya tlanamacato
oipan yohuac ipan ohtli cuac oquitac cente tlatlahuilli omotaya hueca inin oya ic ompa canin oyeya tlatlahuilli oacito ompa open tlapaloa huan nian aquian oquinanquiliaya ocalac ictic cente cauayocalli huan oquitac oyeya miac cauayotlacualli niman inin yocochmiquia
open quitemoa canin cochiz huan oquito   tla aca huallaz nictlaxtlahuiliz tlenon yoquicuauh nocauayo   niman inin yoyaya motecaz iman oquitac cente tlatracualli otlapohtaya ocalac huan oquinextito miac tlacualli open tiotlac tlacua
inin iman yotlacua oce cepa yoquinequia motecaz cuac oquitac cente tlapechtli cuahcualli zan oquihto itic iyollixco omotlahtlani  tlenon nopan mochihua   niman omotecac omomahmalli nochi itzotzoma oquitlati cente icpaltontli niman inin omotecac yocmo oc cepa oizac
momoztlatica oizac oquitemoaya itzotzoma zolhtic yocmo onez oquitac ompo oyeca cente cuahcualli tzotzohraatli omen huan omaqui ion tzotzohmatli yancuic yoyaya iman oquitac tlacualohpechtli open omacehuia otlacua huan ayac oquitaya
nin open quitoa   axan nehua ye nia huan nicmaca miac tlazohcamachi liztli   niman yoquiztaya iman oquitac miac xochime otocataya quihlnamic cuicuiliz cente xochitl quitoa   nehuatl niah nictequiz cente xochitl
iman yoquitec oquiztiz cente yolhcatl huan open quihcahuatza quilhuia   axan niah timitzcuaz   oquihto puchtecatl   amo xinechcua tla xicita nehua onictec inin xochitl zan onechilhui noconen nichuiquiliz cente xochitl
quilhuia yolhcatl   ma amo nimitzcuaz tla ticonanatin moconen ipan yeyi tonaltin ye nican tica tla amo tihuallaz ipan yeyi tonaltin nimitzanatin huan nimitzcuaz
oyaya puchtecatl oacito ichan oyolhmamantaya quitlahtlania cizuonton inon ocachi tzitziquitzin quilhuia   tlenon mitzmaca itlah mitzcocoa itlah oticpolo xinechilhui
oquihto   noconen nian amo nicnequi timitzilhuiz tla xicitta onicalaquito ictic cente calli open quinonotza quenin oipan mochin quilhuia   tehua otinechilhui man timitzotiquiliz cente xochitl onictequito huan ocualan yolhcatl onechilhui tla amo timiztcuicaz nechcuaquin
oquihto cihuonton  tiohue man techcua tonehuan  oyahque oacito huan ayac oquitaya opanoque miac tonaltin quilhuia itata   axan tiah timitzcahuaz nian niquimitatin mocnihuan
oquicahten icecelton huan inin cizuonton oquitlapatiliaya momoztla itlaquen huan amo oquimatia aquin oquitlapatiliaya niman iman yopanoque miac tonalhtin open quicaquiquilhuia   cualli cizuonton nehua nicnequi notlacuaz ca tehuatl   inon oquicaqui itzintla cuahtlatzacualli
inin cizuonton open mamana huan yoquinequia yaz quimitatin itata ca icnihuan iman ce tonalli zan oc huatzinco omen oquitac ompaca cente amatlahcuilolli canin oquilhuitiaya inon yolhcatl man huia ichan man quimitati icnihuan ca itata noihqui oquilhuiaya ipan itzoncuac oyeya ya cente cuahcuahuitl
tla ticnequiz tiaz zan xiquehtzoma inin cuahcuahuitl huan niman mitzhuicaz mochan noihque niman tihuallaz ipan yeyi tonaltin tla amo tihuallaz ipan yeyi tonalhtin tinechnextitin yonimicmellauc zan oquiquehtzoma inon cuahcuahuitl iman oquitac yoyeya ca itata huan ca icnihuan
niman icnihuan amo oquicahque mocuepaz ipan yeyi tonalhtin huan iman omocuep yolhcatl yomic niman open choca cizuonton open quixayacapetzoa quilhuia   tleeca otimic cuahlli yolhcatl
ihqui oquilhuitaya cuac ocochmic niman otlatemic nelli oquilhui yolhcatl   xictequi cente xochitl huan tinechchichipiniliz ipan noixcuac inon atzintli quipia xochitl
niman oixac huan oquitequito xochitl huan oquichichipinili ipan ixcuac niman omehtiquiz inon yolhcatl huan omocuep cente pilhtotontli cuacualtzin huan omozuahtique
ce tiempo coyotl oquimotilito in totatzin dios coquimomaquiliaya licencia para quincuaz nitepilhuan huan oquimotalhui dios  quema siempre que timozahuaz
icuac ino totatzin dios oquimonotzili in tlacuatl para ver de tle modo oquimotlapololtiaya in coyotl     xiauh x namictiuh itech in metlalli huan xilhui cux amo quinequi conitiuh ce quiton necuatl
icuac in coyotl itech in campo oquinamic in tlacuatl omotlapaloque oncan quito in tlacuatl  quen tipano cocoyotzin   in cocoyotzin oquito   cualli tlazocamati
quilhuia tlacuatzin   tiahui nenecuai   otlanananquilia in coyotl  amo porque nehua nozahua porque nitetlanili nitepilhua in dios para niquincuaz
axan oquihto tlacuatlamo tle mopano chihuaz cabo zan atontli toconconizque   amo porque nechitazque dios huan acmo nechmaca nitepilhua para niquincuaz   tlacamo mitzictaz nehua nimitzcamapopoaz
yauh in tlacuatl quitlatlapuz mecomitl huan qui notza in cocoyotzin para atlitiuh    x huallauh ca tli   za ic omopacho in cocoyotzin itech in cuezcomatl para coniz in necuatl za ic zatepan omocani in cocoyotzin oquinotz in tlacuatl para yehua atlitiuh   za ic yuh atlic in tlacuatzin yotemic quinotza in cocoyotzin   x huallauh nimitzcamapopoaz
za ic omopacho in cocoyotzin para quicamapopoazque oc achi oquicamactlaltemi in quilhuia   x camachalo   huan in cocoyotzin icamachaloa za ic tlacuatzin oquicalaquini metzalli itech nitlancochhuan
za ic ye ya tihue itech in campo ihcuac ino ocaqui in coyotl ye quimacatica las doce za ic ye modespediroa de tlacuatzin nizca oya para ichan huan cocoyotzin ye yauh para tetlantzinco n dios uacito omotetlapalhui in dios huan za ic in dios oquimotlatlanili   otimozauh   tlananquilia cocoyotzin   quemacatzin señor   a ver x camachalo
ocamachalo in cocoyotzin nochi nicamac tlatlalhui huan ce metzalli cacticac itech nitlancote ihcuac oquimolhuili n dios   tehua amo timozauh pus axan y acmo nimitzmacaz nopilhua para tiquincuaz axan za nimitzmaca licencia yolcatoton tiquincuaz ichcatoton pitzototon cuanacatoton totoltoton canpa tiquinnamiquiz meno ticalalapuz   za ic ihcuac ino omecuep chocatiuh
oc ce tonalli oquimonamic in tlacuatzin quitua   quen tipano tlatlacuatzin    quitua in tlacuatzin   cualli tlazocamati cocoyotzin  axan nimitzcuaz tleca timonechcacayauh  mopampa amo onozauh axan yacmo nechmaca permiso niquincuaz nitepilhua   lean axan nimitzcuaz
nehua amo cocoyotzin tla timiectin tehua onca nochtlacuatzin onca copalaxtlacuatzin onca necuallacuatzin onca texcallacuatzin   ihcuac ino cocoyotzin oquito  pus vaya tlac amo tehua pus tiahue oncac i tipapacalozque tiahuec ic atlauhco  pus tiahue
huan ihcuac ino oacito atlauhco oquito tlatlacuatzin  anda cocoyotzin nica x quitzqui x tzacuili in texca inter niauh ce mandado nima nimitzpalehuiquiuh pero cuidado quen ticahuahuetziz
cocoyotzin omoyequehuetequitz quintzacuilitica peña para amo huetziz cocoyotzin yociauh quitzcuilitica peña huan tlacuatzin yacmo oc cecpa oacic para quimelahua ce carrera huan quicuepa nixayac in peña zan quenin icatica
oncan zan ic in cocoyotzin oya para ichan oc ce tonalli occecpa omonamique tlatlacuatzin huan cocoyotzin motlapaloque quitoa cocoyotzin   axan za ic mellahuac nimitzcuaz porque tehua zan tinechcacayauhtinemi
nehua amo cocoyotzin tla timiectin tehua onca copalaxtlacuatzin onca nochtlacuatzin onca texcallacuatzin onca necuallacuatzin  tla amo tehua x huallauh topapacalo oncac   tla x ta cocoyotzin niauh nimitzmacaz ce noticia cualca x mozacaticonti ipan nopalli porque axan cualca yauh metlapiltecihuiz
zan ohuatzinco in coyotl yomozacaticonti icpac in nopalle yahue in tlatlacuatzin ica ce coxamitl tetl ihcuac ino peuh quitemotla hast oquitemohui de nopalli   ihcuac ino cocoyotzin otemoc de nopalli tla huel mictihuitz in cocoyotzin quicuaz in tlacuatzin tanto yoquicualani yoquitemohui ica tetl ihcuac ino cocoyotzin yoquitlahuelmicti quilhuia in cocoyotzin tlacuatzin   axan quema mellauh nimitzcuaz tanto yotinechtemotlac hasta yotinechtemohui ica tetl
ay dios cocoyotzin pero pus amo por in omitzilhui timozacaticontiz porque cualca oyaya metlapiltecihuiz    in coyotl tlahuelmicticac   axan amo nimitztlapopolhuia axan za ic nimitzcuaz ihcuac ino omehuitequiz in cocoyotzin icpan tlatlacuatzin ye quinequi quicuaz
icuac ino tlananquilia in tlacuatzin   x quicta cocoyotzin tla tinechcuaz siquier xinechcahuatlallanahuati   tlatlacuatzin opeuh mitotia inter quitztinemi campa ca nitlacoyoc a rato oquictac nitlacoyoc zan oc repente ocalac itech nitlacoyoc yacmo occepa oquiz in cocoyotzin onpo mocauhquichixtiac como tlatlacuatzin acmo occepa oquiz acmo oquinamic occe tonalli
tlen cualle tiquitoz tehua in titetlapololtiani yoyolitl amo xicmoneltoquitican tlen quitoa tla nehuatl i cualle niquixmati huan tehua itec oticalac in cencoatl para mohuilanaz ihuan omitzitlecahui icpac in xochihualcuahitl in nitocan manzana para ic itiquintlapol totatzin adan ihuan eva ic oquicuaque inon xochihualle nicotlatlatoque in ompa paraiso ihuan oquinhualatotocaque in ipan ce choquiz ixtlahuatl
axcan tehua tlen cualle tiquitoz tlacamo omatizquipiaya momaña tlacatecolotl camaxipo mictlan camaventana nenepilmatraca  xiahui xitlacayahua mictlan amo nican tonahuac xia tinemi
huan tla otinechhuicaya tlen otiquitoaya macamo quiquimonequilti no nantzin guadalupana oc tlecan tinelihuicaz xichuica motzonteco
ximochia zantepitzin amo zazan ximapuraro axcan amo nican timocahuaz yi huallaz aquin mitztocaz aquin quitlaliz in motzonteco y acitihuiz amo huecahuaz
acon yon tapohuaya yehua mohuan ne acan niquixmati   llin amatl nechtitlanili ce taco huita nechtazohta icon miacpa nechilia yon ica nicnequi ma nictahuilolino  melahuac nicnequi ma nimonamicti ihuan yon taco nimotahhuaniliti totoca itata   xitequipano ce ome xihuitl ipan llin calli ihuan ihcon titataniz miac mosihuat mitzpalehuis miac tequipanoz mohuan
noyolo ticmati ahuel nimitzelcahua ihuan yon ica aman nimitztahuilolia xicmati yecti tahca ihuan tayohual nimitzpia noixtenco amo xicnechelcahua totoca timotasque chicome aman  xicana ipan moelhuahyo nonamiquiliz ihuan xinechtazohta ac teh quimati
campa tinechmac moyollo ce tayohual ce tonati ni mitztazohta xicmati quen nicnequi mixtelolo itzintan ce tepetontzin campa xochit matechpana nih niquita ce xinola noyolotzin quitilananepa yahui ce tacotzin miac xochit quihualica iten tatahuic quen xochit iten can nicaqui huisa can achi nicmacasquia imanimpa llin tonati ta tohuan tapohuasquia miac nictazohcamati

nican mopohua
nican mopohua motecpana in quenin yancuican huey tlamahuizoltica monexitih in cenquizca ichpochtli santa maria dios inantzin tcuapillahtohcatzin in oncan tepeyacac motenehua guadalupe
achtopa quimottititzinoh ce macehualtzintli itoca juan diego auh zatepan monexitih in itlazohixiptlatzin in iixpan yancuican obispo don fray juan de zumarraga
ye iuh matlacxiuhitl in opehualoc in atl in tepetl mexicco in ye omoman in mitl in chimalli in ye nohuian ontlamatcamani in ahuahcan in tepehuahcan in macazan ye opeuh ye xottla ye cueponi in tlaneltocquiliztli in iiximachocatzin in ipalnemmohuani nelli teotl dios
in huel ihcuac in ipan xiuhitl mil y quinientos y treinta y uno quin iuh iquezquilhuiyoc in metztli diciembre mochiuh oncatca ce macehualtzintli icnotlapaltzintli itoca catca juan diego iuh mihtoa ompa chaneh catca in cuauhtitlan auh in ica teoyotl oc mochompa pouhiya in tlatelolco auh sabado catca huel oc yohuatzinco quihualtepotztoccaya in teoyotl ihuan in inetihtitlaniz
auh in ahcico in inahuac tepetzintli in itocayocan tepeyacac ye tlatlalchipahua concac in icpac tepetzintli cuiccohua iuhquin nepapan tlazohtotomeh cuiccah cacahuani in intozqui iuhquin quinahnanquilia tepetl huel cenca teyolquima tehhuellamachtia in incuic quicempanahuia in coyoltototl in tzinitzcan ihuan in occequin tlazohtotometh in cuiccah
quimotztimoquetz in juan diego quimolhuih cuix nolhuil cuix nomacehual in ye niccaqui azo zan nictemiqui azo zan nicochitlehua canin ye ticah canin ye ninotta cuix ye oncan in quihtohtehuanqueh huehuetqueh tachtohuan tocohcolhuan inxochitlalpan intonnacayotlapan cuix ye oncan in ilhuicatlalpan

huel nicnequi cenca niquelehuia inic nican nechquechiliz

auh inic huel neltiz in nicnemilia in notehicnoittaliz ma xiauh in ompa in itecpanchan in mexicco obispo auh tiquilhuiz in quenin nehuatl nimitztitlani inic tiquixpantiz in quenin huel cenca niquelehuia inic in nican nechcalti nechquechili in ipan in tlalmantli noteocal huel moch ticpouhiliz in ixquich in otiquittac oticmahuizoh ihuan in tlein oticcac
auh ma iuh ye in moyolloh ca huel nictlazohcamatiz auh ca niquixtlahuaz ca ic nimitzcuiltonoz nimitztlamachtiz ihuan miec oncan ticmacehuaz ic niccuepcayotia in mociauhiliz in motlatequipanoliz inic ticnemilitiuh in tlein nimitztitlani
o ca ye oticcac noxocoyouh in nihiyo in notlahtol ma ximohuiccatiuh ma ixquich motlapaltililiz xicmochiuhili

quihuicaltiaya in totolin in ipan tetlamacaya tlani quitlaliaya molcaxic in chichinacatl zan pani quitlaliaya in totolnacatl in tetech monequia
auh niman yehoatl in cacahuatl quinextiaya azo cen tecpan xiquipilli in tetech monequi
auh niman yehoatl quinextiaya in acacuauhitl azo macuiltzontli azo matlac tzontli
niman yehuatl in molcaxitl in chiquihuitl in zoquitecomatl in puchtecayo caxitl in cuahuitl in tecolli mochi quicaltema
niman yehoatl quipatiyotia in atl in cecem ilhuitl popolihuia azo ye acalli anozo nauh acalli in cem acalli ipatiuh catca centetl in tecuachtli momacaya
in centetl tecuachtli ipatiuh catca macuil pohualli in cacahuatl yehuatl in tototlacualtecuachtli
auh in quitoquilia huel yehuatl in tecuachtli napohualli ipatiuh catca in cacahuatl
auh zan ye quene tlatzacuia tecuachtli e pohualli on macuilli cacahuatl ipatiuh catca
auh in ye yuhqui in o tlacencauh ye mochi nez ixquich omoteneuh in omito niman ye onpehua in tochtepec in ompa cem onoque in puchteca in oztomeca in ye nohuian altepetl ipan in ye nohuian altepetl ipan tlaca oncan cem onoca in ical
centetl ic catcain tenochtitlan in tlatilolco in tetzcoco in huexotla in cohuatl ichan in chalco in xochimilco in huitzilopuchco in mixcohuac in azcapotzalco in cuauhtitlan in otompan
in ic motlayecoltitinenca in nohuian altepetl ipan calactinenca zan oncan huallacuepaya in tochtepec
auh in altepehuaque amo huel calacque in anahuac zan iyoque in calaquia in mexica in tenochca in mexica tlatilolca inhuicalhuan catca in cuauhtitlan calque ihuan huitzilopochca
auh in oacito tochtepec in yehuatl tealtiz niman ye ic calaqui in ichan tlatilulca quimamalia in quitetlauhtiz ihuan in acacuahuitl
niman ye ixpan tlamelahua in oncan ca in teuh in oztoxneca itoca iyacatecutli
iciuhtica tlachpana ixpan conteca petlatl in ocontecac niman ye ic quixintiniz in itlaquen yeticac in yacatecutli
niman ye ic quitotoma in otlatopilii intla ce intia ome intla yey intla nahui caltiz izqui conana yehuatl in huel cualli in huel xocpale
auh in oconan niman ye ic quihilpia conquetza in oncan hicaya conquentia in tlatquiyeticac in amatl ixpan contema petlapan in otlatopilli
auh in ic tealtiz oncan quitemachitia intla ome caltiz ce oquichtli ce cihuatl auh intla nahui caltiz ome oquichtli ome cihuatl
auh in intech quitealizque in tilmatli yehuatl in coyoichcatl tetecomayo ihuitica tenchilnahuayo
ihuan in mextlatl yacahuiac ihuan cueyitl tetenazcayo chicocueyitl ihuan huipilli xochimoyahuac anozo xoxoloyo
mochi oncan contlalia in ixpan iyacatecutli in ic oncan ittoz in iuhqui intech quitlalizque tlaltilli oncan ca quitemahuizoltiaya in ic teyoluaia
auh in ocontlali niman ye ic calaqui in calitic oncan cate tlatilulca
niman ic tlanahuatia iciuhca mochihua in tlacualli in totolin in cacahuatl
auh in omocencauh in ixquich tetech monequi niman ye ic tenotzalo quinnotza in oztomeca in tealtianime in tecohuanime matlactepetl omome quinotzaya yohualnepantla in calaquia
auh in ocenquizato in ye mochi tlacatl niman ye ic tematequilo in on tematequiloc niman ye ic tetlamaco
tlacualo auh in on tlacualoc ye no ceppa tematequilo tecamapaco niman ye ic teamaco teyemaco zatepan tetlauhtilo
auh in tecencauh in tealtiz niman ye ic yauh in tlenamacaz quitquilia in zollin
intla ome caltiz ontetl zolin in quimictia auh intla ey intla nahui caltiz izquitetl zolin quimictia
ompa ixpan on moquetza in tletl niman ye conquechcotona in zolin icama contlaza in tletl
niman ye ic tlenamaca nappa in coniyahua in tonatiuh iquizayan nauhcampaixti yuh quichihuaya
auh in ye yuhqui in on tlenamacac niman ye ic teixpan on motlalia ce tlacatl itech mocahua
yehuatl quitlatlalhuia quitlatauhtilia quitohua
ca oticenquizaco in ye tixquich in ye timochin in tahua in titepehua in tipuchtecatl in toztomecatl
in nican tiquihiyohuico in ticciahuico in tonehuaco in chichinacaco in moyollo in monacayo in tinocuauh in tinocelouh in ticuauhtlacatl in tizacatlacatl in titoxonqui in tihuazonqui
in ah tictlazotla in melchiquiuh in motzontecon in ic ticmotla in texcalli in atlauhtli in ixtlahuatl
can ca in tictemohua in itotonca in iyamanca in tloque nahuaque
auh iz catqui ipatiuh in atlauhtli in tepetl in ixtlahuatl ma cana on tlapolo ma cana temac contlaz in iaxcatzin in itlaquitzin in tlacatl toteuyo
auh ca ixco icpac on tlachiaznequi in tlacatl in tetzahuitl in huitzilopuchtli cetzin concotoniliznequi in icococauh in icocouh
ca ixquich in ticmocuilia ic pachihuia in moyollotzin in tahua in titepehua in tipuchtecatl in toztomecatl
auh niman ye ic quicuepa in tlatolli in puchteca tlatoque in izquintin cecen altepetl ipan tlapachohua teyacana quitohua
totecohuan e pochteca ye ca nican anmonoltitoque ca otoconanque ca otoconcuique in choquiztli in ixayotl ca otocontlapoque in toptli in petlacalli in oilpitoca in otzauhctoca in ipatiuh in cuauhtli in ocelotl
ca nican tontiachia ipaltzinco in tlacatl totecuyo in tloque nahuaque otech mocnelili auh in ye ixquich
niman ye ic tlanahuatia in ichan puchteca niman ye ic hualpehua quitquitihui in ihuitopil yez
auh in oacico in ichan in nican mexico tlatilolco niman iciuhca concencahua in itech monequiz in puchteca tlatoque in nahualoztomeca
zan oc eintin in quincaquitia cuappoyahualtzin huuetzcatotzin zanatzin quintlacualtia quimatlitia quimiyemaca quintlauhtia

auh in oquimocencauh niman ye imixpan on motlalia quimilhuiapipiltzitzine namech notlalcahualtiliz namech notlapololtiliz
ca izcatqui anquimanilia anquimocuilia ca ixco icpac nontlachiaznequi in tetzahuitl in huitzilopochtli
an ca cana cetzin omonexiti in icococauh in tlacatl totecuyo
cana nontlapoloz nontlatoctiz nontlachitoniz ca ic pachihuia in amoyollotzin
niman ye ic quitlatlauhtia quilhuia telpochtl e ca nican tica ac tehuantin ac titomati in nican tictlapohua in itop in ipetlacal in tlacatl totecuyo in tetzahuitl in huitzilopochtli
ca nican ticcaqui in mochoquiz in motlaocol in ye macuil in ye matlac in ye ce xiuh in ye oxxiuh ic timotequipachotinemi
azo zan mococoneyo micnopillo timaitia ma aoncan tinen acazomo titenamic ma ahuel ticchiuh
ma zan tontlapinauhti ma titechpinauhti in puchteca in oztomeca in iyaque in tealtianime in tecohuanime
acazomo achtopa o ic titlatecac otitlacencauh in ixquich tetech monequi ma tontlachiecan in topco in petlacalco ca nel yehuatl in ic tihuehuetque
niman ye ic quinpohuilia in ixquich omoteneuh in popolihuiz
in o inyollo on pachiuh niman ye ic quilhuiatelpochtl e ca otocon tlachielique in tloque nahuaque nel iyolic xi moquetza ma momamimic ma mocximimic
ma titlacuecuetlaxo ma timozotlauh ihuan ma itla ilihuiz tiquito motlatol ma ticiuhca tlato iyolic temac xon otiuh
ca ic timitz yolpachiutia    ca nappa in titetlacualtiz in ic ceppa in titeyolmelahuaz     in ic oppa ihcuac in tontlaixnextiz     in ic expa ihcuac in tetehualtiz     in ic nappa ihcuac in titlamictiz
ma cana oncan tic elehui in teaxca in tetlatqui achtopa timitz machitia
ye no ceppa quimilhuia piltzitzine oannech mocnelilique otlaocox in amoyollotzin azo cana nocontlazaz in amihiyotzin in amotlatoltzin 
ma xicmitalhuiacan in quen conequiz in amoyollotzin ma cacoqui ma cuihualoqui ma analoqui in amotenanyotzin in amotetayotzin
niman ye quilhuia ca ye cualli xole ma oc ticpohuacan in cualli tonalli
niman ic tlaihua connotza in tonalpouhqui zan icatca in tetonalpohuiliaya oncan motlayecualtiaya
auh in oconittac in cualli tonalli in cemilhuitl techitquia niman quitoa ma ihcuac ni cecalli anozo omexochitl anozo omeozomatli in zazo catlehuatl canaz cualli tonalli
uel ipan in conpehualtia in itequipachol in yehoatl tealtiz
auh in o inyollo onpachiuh in puchteca huehuetque zan ic cen connahuatia quilhuia
ca nican tica nopiltze xole ca o toyollo on pachiuh ca otoconanque ca otoconcuique in mochoquiz in monetequipachol
ma ic tatlama ma ic timopouh ma ic teixco teicpac tinen

ye ixquich in tonequixtil mochihua

auh in oquimoncencauhque yohualnepantla achtopa quintlacualtia quimatlitia

auh in ic oppa tenotzaya ihcuac in on tlaixneztia zan no yuh mochihuaya in omito
auh in ic expa tenotzaya ihcuac in tetehualtia ihcuac quimonaqui aya imicpac in tlaltiluan mitohuaya anecuyotl

cuicuicaliz tlahtulli
in aquin cuicuicaya ihcuac in ye miec iaxca italtqui in ye quitta in inecuiltonul inetlamachtil in ye oquitlaoculli totecuiyo
niman ye ic moyolnonotza ye quitoa ca izcatqui in onech motlaoculili in totecuiyo in tlalticpaque in tloque nahuaque in icococauh in iaxcatzin in italtquitzin
ma moztla ma huiptla nechmotlaoculili in totecuiyo ma noce nitlapolo ma ni tlatocti ma nitlachitonilli in tlacatl in tocuiyo
auh ma ixco ma icpac nitlachie in icnohuehue in icnoilama auh in tonanuan in totahuan in pochteca huehuetque in puechteca tlahtoque
auh in cetzin omehtzin in motolinia in icnotlaca in nohuainyolque ma ni quin centlali ma oc niquin moniximati

quitohua nopiltzine nican catqui macatzin

auh niman yehuatl quitoquilia in xochitl in ic quitqui imayauhcampa in quitzitzquia in chimalxochitl auh iopochcopa ompa quitziztquia in cuauhxochitl
ipampa in ompa quitzitzquia imayauhcan ca in yehuatl in xochimaco ca quixnamictimoquetza in texochimacac auh in ic qui hual cuilia in chimalxochitl iyopochcopa
auh in imayauhcan ompa qui hual cui in cuauhxochitl in yehuatl in in chimalxochitl quinezcayotia in chimalli
auh niman yehuatl quitoquilia in tlacualli in ic quitqui imayauhcampa quitzitzquia in mulcaxitl amo itenco in quitzitzquia zan imacpal nepantla quimantiuh

auh in yehuantin pochteca tlahtoque ahmo mihtotia zan onoque mopixtoque ipampa ca yehuantin in tecohuachihua

 in ic pochtecatia in quinmacaya zan yehuatl in cuezali ihuan cuitlatexotli ihuan chamoli zan in ye tlamaniztli in ic pochtecatitiaque
 auh in ic ome motlalico tlatohuani tlacateotl auh no ipan motlalique in pochtecatlahtoque yehuantin in cozmatzin tzompantzin ye impan nez in quetzalli ayamo huiac ihuan zacuan ihuan xihuiti ihuan chalchihuitl ihuan yamanqui tilmahtli yamanqui maxtlatl in nequentiloya zan oc mochi ichtilmatzintli ichuipiltzintli ichcuetzintli

 auh ye impan nez in teocuitlatentetl ihuan in teocuitlanacochtli ihuan maxitlaztli yehuatl in motocayotia matzatzaztli anilla ihuan chayahuac cozcatl teocuitlatl teoxihuitl ihuan huehuey chalchihuitl ihuan huiac quetzalli ihuan tecuanehuatl ihuan huiac zacuan ihuan xiuhtototl ihuan teoquechol

 auh in tenochtitlan tlahtocati in ahuitzotzin ye ipan in calacque pochteca ayotlan in anahuac ompa impan hualmotzaoc nauhxihuitl in caltzaoctimanca in cuauhtenanco

 auh ye oncan monahuatique in ic mocentlalique quihtoque

 auh in omotlali ahuitzotzin niman ye ic qui tlamahmaca in ixquich malli omochiuh in quetzalpatzactli quetzalpanitl zacuampanitl xiutotoehuatl tzinitzcan ehuatl machoncotl xiuhchimalli teocuitlayacapapalotl teocuitlanacaztepoztli in ixpan contequilique

 ma intlaxcahuil intonehuiliz in chichinaquiliz omochiuh ma intlahcuiuh ma xoconmocuili
 auh niman quimilhui notlatzitzinhuan e oanquihiyohuique oanquiciauhque oqui monequilti in tlacatl in tetzahuitl in huitzilopochtli in o huel anquichiuhque amotequiuh auh nican amixco amocpac nitlachie
 ca iz catqui in amocococauh in amelchiquiuh in amotzontecon ipatiuh omochiuh ayac amech cahualtiz ca nel amaxca amotlatqui ca oan qui mahcehuato
 auh niman quin macac in tilmahtli amanepaniuhqui tempapaloyo ihuan tilmahtli tetecomayo ihuan temalacayo ihuan nochpallaxochyo chichicueezotl ihuan nochpalmaxtlatl yacahuiac

 auh in ixquich omoteneuh in tlahuiztli in quetzalpatzactli mochi commaquique in pochteca in ipan ompeuhque huel quimpopoloque

 auh in yehuantin in pochtecatlahtoque in nahualoztomeca in teyahualoni yaoc calaquini oc cenca oquin mahuizzoti teocuitlatentetl quimonaquili intenco in ic quin nezcayoti yehuantin in teucnenencahuan omochiuhque
 auh in tlazotilmahtli quin macac in omoteneuh ihuan tlazomaxtlatl in innetlauhtil mochiuh quin ihcuac quimolpiliaya in ihcuac huehuey ilhuitl quiztihuia in ipan tlacaxipehualiztli
 yeh ihcuac hual cemolinia in cematonahuac hual mocehmacia in nican mexico in ilhuitl qui hual quiztiaya ce xiutica in qui hual mattihuia auh ye ixquich in omocemaaco tlahtoque in quipachohua altepetl
 niman ye ic ompehua in ic tlahuahuanoz temalacac huel in ixpan mochihuaia huel quimittaya in quizquitzontli mamaltin miquia
 auh no huel quimittaya in aquin amo yollo chicahuac no huel quimittaya in cequintin oc achiton ic hual tetlamahuizoltia hual moquichnenenqui cequintin oc hual mihtotia
 auh in yehuantin tlahtoque in qui motlauhtiaya yehuatl in tlatocatilmahtli tehtecomayo xahualcuauhyo ihuan tlauhquechol yehcacehuaztli in quin motlauhtiaya in ixquichtin quipachohuaya altepetl in tlahtoque
 auh in ihcuac tlahuahuano oncan ic mocehualuitoque
 auh in zan nenmayan in amo ilhuitl in quimolpiliaya tilmahtli in pochteca tlahtoque in tealtiani auh in nahualoztomeca in tecohuanime za yehuatl in iczotilmahtli xixipetztli mochipa yehuatl quiquentinemia
 auh pipiltin zan no ihcuac in quimilpilitihuia in tlazotilmahtli in mahuiztic in ihcuac izquitetl huehueyi ilhuitl quiztihuia in ic taci ce xihuitl
 auh in ihcuac nenmanyan in amo ilhuitl zan no yehuatl in iczotilmahtli xixipetztli in quimulpiliaya zan quinamictihuia in netlalpilil
 ipampa in cenca mihmatia pipiltin cenca tlanemiliani catca
 auh in ihcuac tlanahuatiaya ahuitzotzin in campa calaquizque in pochtecatlahtoque in nahualoztomeca in teyaohualohuani iaoc quin hual notzaya in ahuitzotzin yehuantin concaqui in itlatul in ipampa teocnehnemoaz in anahuac
 auh in oyaque ichan tlahtohuani ahuitzotl teoctli niman ye ic quin maca in itlatqui nauhtzontli in cuachtli in quin tiamictia
      auh in oconcuito nican quihualitque tlatilolco auh in ohuallaque niman ic mocentlalia in tenochca pochteca ihuan tlatilolca pochteca
 mocepan tlahtlauhtia quiquiztia in imihiyo in intlatul in intlacazaz caltiliz in intlacahuapahualiz
 auh in ye iuhqui in ommotlatlauhtique in onmocepan chicahuaque niman ye ic qui hual moxelhuia on tzontli concui in cuachtli tenochca auh no on tzontli concui in tlatilolca
 auh in cuachtli niman ic mocohua in tlahtocatilmahtli ihuitica tetecomayo ihuan xahualcuauhyo tilmahtli ihuan ihuitica tenehuahuanqui ihuan tlahtocamaxtlatl yacahuiac ihuan tlamachcueyitl tlamachuipilli
 inin tlatquitl huel ixcoya iaxca in ahuitzotzin in quitquiliaya anahuac pochteca
 auh iz catqui in zan imixcoya intlatqui pochteca in ic oztomacati on teocnehnemi tepeyo teocuitlatl iuhquin tlatocayotl ihuan teocuitla ixcuamatl ihuan chayahuac cozcatl teocuitlatl ihuan teocuitlanacochtli ihuan teocuitlatl tzacualoni intech monequi in anahuacacihua
 yehuantin in cihuapipiltin ic quitzacua in innacayo ihuan in maxitlaztli in itoca matzatzaztli ihuan teucuitlanacochtli ihuan tehuilonacochtli
 auh in zan macehualtin intech monequi yehuatl in itznacochtli tepoznacochtli ihuan amochitl ihuan itztlaehualli neximaloni ihuan huitzauhqui itztli ihuan tochomitl ihuan huitzmallotl ihuan coyolli
 ixquich in in ic mochichihuaya in imixcoya intlatqui in pochteca in oztomeca in teocnenenque
 auh in ihcuac in ye ompehuazque niman ye quitemohua in cualli tonalli yehuatl in cecohuati ohtli melahuac anozo cecipactli anozo ceozomatli anozo chicomecohuatl
 in omotonalpohuique oztomeca yehuantin quimati in ca tlehuatl ipan onpehuazque
 auh in ihcuac in ye moztla on ehuazque in ipan cualli tonalli niman ye ic mahmohuia moxima in nican mexico zan ic cen
 auh in ixquich cahuitl nemitihui anahuac aic ceppa mahmohuia moxima zan yo moquechaltia amo polaqui ixquich cahuitl mozauhtinemia
 auh in oyohuac in oacic tlahtlapitzalizpan niman ye ic quipehualtia in amaxotla
 achtopa quitequi in itech pohui in tletl quitohuaya xiuteoctli tlalxictentica auh in amatl quitequia tlayopitectli iuhquin cuachpanitl ic tlatectli
 quitlahcoilpia tlauhtica ic caltia in oconcencauhque niman ye oltica quihcuilohua
 auh in ic quicuilohua in olli ic quizo coyolomitl niman ye ic contlecuinaltia tlatlatinemi in ic tlahcuilohua
 auh in ic quicuilohua amatl quitentia quiyacantia quixtelolotia iuhquin in tlacatl ic tlachie in ic quixiptayiotia tletl
 niman yehuatl quitequi in itech pohui tlalli quitoahuaya tlalteoctli amatica tlaelelpilli no oltica quitentia quiyacatia quihixtelololtia no yuhquin tlacatl tlachie
 niman yehuatl quitequi in itech pohui in yacateoctli in cocohcohimetl iyacapitzahuac yehuatl in otlatopilli quicencuitlalpiaya huel yehuatl in quimoteotiaya in pochteca in oztomeca in campa huia
 in campa caiaquia oztomecatizque quitquitihui in intopil auh in amatl itech pohuiya tlanautzontectli oltica tlapeyahualli
 niman yehuatl quitequi in itech pohui ce cohuatl ohtli melahuac in ic quitequi zan no ye in tlanauhtzontectli in ic quihcuilohua amatl oltica quicohuaihcuilohua quitlalia in itzontecon ihuan ixtelolo quicamatia quinenelpitia quicuechtia
 niman yehuatl quitequi in itech pohui in tlacotzontli in zacatzontli in ic quitequi amatl zan tzinpapalotic auh in ic talcuilolli zan tlaolchipinilli
 auh in oconcencauhque niman ye ic muxtlahua in yohualnepantla achtopa oncan ixpan quimanilia in tetl itech pohui
 niman ye ic quiza in ithualnepantla oncan contecpana in inextlahual in itech pohui tlalli quitoahuaya tlalteoctli ihuan ce cohuatl in yehuatl in ohtli melahuac ihuan tlacotzontli zacatzontli
 auh in yacateoctli inemac conquentia in otlatopilli aic tlatla in amatl in izquipan moxtlahua zan mochipa conquentia
 auh in ye yuhqui in o mochi centecpanque in inextlahual ithualnepantla niman ye ic calaqui in inchan ixpan moquetza in tletl oncan conquechcotona in zoli
 in oconquechcoton niman ye ic huitzauhqui ic quizo in innacaz anozo in inenepil in quizo
 in ihcuac ye quiza eztli imatica concui quitohuaya teonauhpa in contlaza tleco niman ye ic ipan quichichipitza in amatl in oipan ommihzoc
 niman ye ic hual quiza in ithualnepantla achtopa on tlatlaza in ilhuicac contlaza in iezzo
 niman ye ompa in tonatiuh iquizaya mihtohuaya tlapcopa nauhpa in contlaza iezzo
 niman ye ompa in tonatiuh icalaquian mitohuaya cihuatlan no nauhpa in contlaza iezzo
 niman ye ompa in imaopochcopa tlalli mihtohuaya huitznahuaca tlalli no nauhpa in contlaza iyezzo
 niman ye ompa in imayauhcanpa tlalli mihtohuaya mimixcohua in tlalpan no nauhpa in contlaza iyezzo za ompa ommocahua in ic nauhcampa ommihzo
 auh in ye iuhqui onmizoc in oconquixti in iezzo no ipan conchichipitza in amatl oncan mani itualnepantla in ommihzo
 niman ye no ceppa calaqui in ichan ixpan moquetza in tletl niman ye ic concui in amatl cahcocui nauhpa in coniahua in ihuicpa tletl quilhuia in ic quinotza
 ma xi mehuiltitie moceloquichtle tlalxictenticae nauhyotecutle ma ihuian xichual manili momocauh in maxcatzin azo itla o ic nimitznoyolitlacaihui
 niman ye ic conmana in amatl in tleco in oconman zatepan concui in iztac copalli yehuatl in tzihuac copalli in huel melahuac in huel yaque in huel chipahuac in amo tlazollo in amo teuhyo
 niman itlan conaqui in amatl in ic huel cuetlaniz auh huel quitztimoquetza in ic tlatla huel quimocuitlahuiticac
 in tla zan ye pochehua in amatl amo huel tlatla cenca momauhtiaya oncan quittaya in ahzo cana cuculliztli quicuitiuh
 auh intla iciuhca tlatla in cenca cocomoca cuecuetlaca ic cenca papaqui iitic quitohua
 o nechmocnelili in tlacatl totecuyo ca huel nahciz in ompa niauh
 auh in ye yuhqui niman ye ic quiza in itualnepantla in oncan mani amatl
 niman ye ic concui ompa itztimoquetza in tonatiuh iquizayan no nauhpa in coniahua nauhcampaixti iuh quichihua
 auh in ic concui amatl achtopa quicui in itech pohui in tlacotzontli niman yehuatl in itech pohui zacatzontli niman yehuatl in itech pohui cecoatl hotli melahuac
 zan pani quimana quicennapalohua in ic conmana tleco in oncan itualco
 in on tlatlac niman ye ic tlatataca in zan no oncan itualnepantla oncan quicentoca in calitic otlatlac amanextli zan quizololohua amo no ye in tleco nextli
 ihui in mochihuaia yohualtica auh in ohualatuic niman ye ic tlatitlani tlaihua in quimonnotza in pochtecatlahtoque quincentlalia in ixquichtin pochteca nahualoztomeca in tealtiani in tecohuani
 auh in telpochnemi huel ixquichtin quincentlalia in ilamatque in ihuanyolque in cihuatzitzintin in iiahuian
 auh in ocenquizque niman ye ic temahtequilo tecamapaco in on tematequiloc niman ye ic tetlamaco
 in on tlacualoc ye no ceppa temahtequilo tecamapaco niman ye ic teamaco atlihua niman ye yeti temaco
     auh in ye yuhqui niman ye ixpan motlalia quintlatlauhtia quimilhuia
 o anquimociahuiltique o anquihiyohuiltique ca nican cententica cencamatica nictlatlauhtia in amotenanyotzin in amotehtayotzin
 ca oc ye nocontlalcahuia in amaxochtzin in amotlaxilacaltzin auh in amatzin in amotepetzin
 ma oc nichual chihua in temahtequiliztli in tecamapaquiliztli in zacapepechtzintli ca omonexiti in tlahcohcohualtzintli in iztlaehualtzintli in coyoltzintli in huitzmallotzintli in nocheztzintli in tlalxocotzintli
 azo huel nechon mohtlatoctiliz in tloque nahuaque ca yehuatl in anquimocuilia in anquimocaquitia
 auh in ihcuac o yuh quimilhui niman ye ic quicuepilia in itlatol in pochtecatlahtoque in izquipetlame in ic cecencalpulpan teyacana
 pochtlan ahuachtlan atlauhco acxotlan tepetitlan itztulco tzonmolco inin chicuacen petlame cecenme teyacanque tlapachohua
 in ihcuac campa tlacamacho in cohuanotzalo in ic onoque tecpantoque tlayahualotoque centlapal incal mayetica in pochteca tlahtoque auh no centlapal incal mayetica in nahualoztomeca in yaopan teyahualoni zan tlatzaoctoque tecpantoque in telpupochtin
 auh in yehuatl teyacantica in pochtecatlahto yacattiuh in quitlatlauhtia quilhuia
 ca ye cualli ca nican tica ca otoconanque ca otoconcuique auh ca otoconcacque in mihiyo in motlatol
 ma iyolic xocon ana mocxi ca ye toconnamiquiz in cecohuatl ohtli meiahuac
 ma cana toconicxinamic in in tecohuatl in cuauhcohuatl in tlacotzontli in zacatzontli
 ma iyolic xocon toca in teotlalli in ixtlahuatl azo cana mitzpopoloz in totec in tloque nahuaque in ilhuicahua in tlalticpaque
 ma cana xi popolihui cuahuiti itic texcalli itic ma onca huilanto in mayazultzin in momaxtlazultzin
 ma cana cecemanto momiyotzin auh in motzontzin ma cana momoyahuato in teiyocan in tocayehcan
 ma ompa popouhto ma ompa ixtlauto in icnopillotl in icnotlacayotl
 auh intla ca can huel mitzpopuhloz mitztlahtlatiz in tlacatl in totecuyo ma hual timalihui in ah cococ in ah poyec in itztayotzintli in tlaolpahuatzintli
 auh no ihuan ma cana tontezoquimotla tonteatlatzicuinalui xi moteimacaxili xi motemauhcaittili
 intla ye itla ticpielia in itotonca in iyamanca in tloque nahuaque ma mitznacaztlachielti
 azo cana tontenepanohua tocohuapan azo tenochtitlan azo cuauhtitlan azo azcapotzalco azo huitzilopochco huel motlatolti cualli ic xi motenochili
 auh intla huel itech tahciz in altepetl in ompa titlamattiuh ma xocon cuitihuetzi in tepoztli in cuauhtequiliztli in tlachpanaliztli in tletlaliliztli in tlahuiliztli in tlatzehtzeloliztli in tematequiliztli in tecamapaquiliztli
 auh in ixquich in tlamacehualiztli in acxoyacuihualiztli ye ixquich in tic caqui
 in aquin iuh quicentlaliaya in in pochteca tlahtoque in izquipetlame yehuatl in ye otlacnopilhui in ye miec iaxca itlatqui
 auh in zan oc motolinia in ayamo cenca miec iaxca itlatqui zan oc icalpultian in quin notza pochteca oztomeca
 auh in aquin tachcauhchiuhtiaz amo zan icel in quin nonotzaya in quin caquia tlahtolli mochintin in quin huicaz in quezquintin moyolehuaya
 in cequintin quin in yopa yazque azo quin telpochtepitoton in quintehuicaltiaya in intahuan in innanuan
 quitoaya ma tehuica in telpochtontli in cuautla in zacatla in teniyocan in tocayecan
 ca ompa mani in tezcatl ca ompa hicac in tlahuilli in ocotl ca ompa in atl cecec in tzitzicaztli
 azo ompa tepal tlachiez mozcaliz tlacaquiz ma ompa pohpolihui tleh nel aiz tleh nel nicchihuaz cuix cihuatl azo malacatl tzotzopaztli imac nictequiliz 
 auh in yehuatl tetatzin tenantzin zan ixcoyan in quitlatlauhtia in impiltzin quilhuia
 ca nican tica nopiltze notelpochtze nocenteconetzine timotolinia tle nel taiz tleh ticchihuaz ca o ic mitzmochihuili in tlacatl totecuio in tloque nahuaque in tlalticpaque in ic toquichtli
 ma ihuian xon motehuiquilitiuh ma tetech xocon itztiuh in iuh huilohua in iuh otlatoco
 auh yuh teixpan manalo in mulcaxitl in chiquihuitl in iuh teamaco huel xi motlachielti in catlehoatl achtopa mocui in ic teixpan nequetzalo huel xicmottili in iuh tlatecpano
 auh in ihcuac in ye yazque in ye onpehuazque achtopan ichan monechicohua in aquin teyacanaz in tachcauhtiaz
 mochi oncan mocen nechicohua in ixquich tlamamalli in tiamictli ihuan in ixquich tetlatquitilli in imaxca in pochteca tlahtoque
 ihuan in intlatqui pochteca cihua nononcua mochichihua huel ixpan mochintin oncan mocentlalitoque oncan cenquiztoque
     quichizticate in quenman onpehuazque auh mochi quinechicohua in ihtacatl in pinolli auh in quicaltema amo cemilhuitl zan yohualtica
 auh in ihcuac ocenquiz in ye mochi tlamamalli niman ye ic quichichihua cacaxtica quiquehquetza in tlaquehualtin quimamazque achi etic zan quipantia
 auh in yehuantin quimamazque in pochteca amo cenca etic zan tlaeheculli zam mochiuhqui
 auh no ic momana in tachcauhchiuhtiazque in quiya canazque tlamamalli
 auh in quin ihopa yazque in telpochtepitoton aya tle quimamaltia zan oc yehuatl in atlihualoni quimamaltia in ayotectli
 auh in ihcuac otlatecpanque in calihtic in iuh huilohuaz hotlica in on yohuac in ye tlapoyahua niman ye ic tlacaltemalo in acalli azo ontetl anozo yetetl in ic yauh tlatquitl
 in ye yuhqui in on tlacaltemaloc niman ye ic tlanahuatia in ye onmacalaquizque teixpan on motlalia quitohua
 ca nican ammoyetzticate piltzitzine amocxitzin cehcepoatin ma oc tamechtotlaluilican ma oc tonyatihuian
 ca o tic cuique ca oc tic anque in amihiyotzin in amotlahtultzin in amoxillantzinco in amotozcatlatzinco cuel pachiuhtia in ilpiltica
 in choquizzo in tlaocollo ma oc tic tlalcahuican in quiahuatl in ithualli auh in tahui in tohueltiuh in tocotonca in tohuiltecca   ma cuele techilcahua
 auh niman ye ic quincuepilia in intlatul quimilhuia
 ca ye cualli ma iyolic xocon anacan in amocxi maca tle xichual mattihuia in amocalihtic in amotlecuillan
 ca miec in oanquicacque in nanyotl in tahyotl in ic o amihilpiloque in teyo in cuauhyo in atl itztic cecec tzizticatztli amotech opachiuh
 ma cana anquitlahxiliti anquinchitoniliti in imihiyo in intlatol in amonanhuan in amotahuan
 auh motolinia in amomatitech anquimonantihui in telpopochtzitzintin ma contetlalilihtihuian in teicpaltzintli in xiuhpepetzintli in zacaicpaltzintli
 auh in ixquich in tlamacehualiztli in yohualtamachihualiztli in ixtozzoliztli
 xi quin cuitlahuiltican xi quin tlacuauhtzitzquiltican ma anquizxiccauhti in huapahualoni in izcaltiloni
 ihui in iz ca ic cen quinnahuatiaya in on tzonquiz tlahtulli niman ye ic nequetzalo ye omotlali in cenca huey tletl xoxohuic copalxialli ixpan mani
 cehceyaca concuitimani in copalli contentimani in tleco niman ic quiz timani acalco tlamelahua
 aoc ac calaqui cihuapan ha no ac hual mocuepa ma hual nacaztlachie
 in azo itia oquilcauhtia in ma oc concuique in ma nozo conmacati aocmo hueliti
 ha no ac quintocatiuh in ixquich tlacatl pochteca huehuetque pochteca cihua
 in aquin hual mocuepaya quitetzauhmatia quitlahtlaculmatia cohuicattaya
 iuhqui in in ic onpehuaya in oztomeca

 in tlazotilmahtli in tlazocueyitl in tlazohuipilli in iaxcan ahuitzotzin in ic quimontlapalohua
 auh in o quimonmacaque niman ye ic quihualcuepcayotia in anahuatlahtoque
 yehuatl ihuiac quetzalli ihuan totocuitlapiltic quetzalli ihuan chilchotic quetzalli ihuan xiuhtototl ihuan tzinitzcan
 auh in ompa calaquia anahuac amo mochi tlacatl icalaquian catca ipampa ca icohuapan catca in ahuitzotzin
 zan iyoque in ompa huia in ompa calaquia in tlatilolca tenochca huitzilopochca azcapotzalca cuauhtitlan calque zan mochipa yehuantin in huicalhuan mochiuhtinenca
 in ihcuac in ye onpehua anahuac pochteca oncan moxelohuaya in tochtepec centlamantli ompa calaquia in anahuac ayotlan no centlamantli ompa calaquia anahuac xicalanco
 auh in ic motequimacaya occam moxelohuaya in tlatilolca no occam moxelohuaya in tenochca in ihuihuicalhuan in huitzilopochca in azcapotzalca in cuauhtitlan caique
      auh in ic ohtlatocaya moyaochichiuhtihuia in inchimal inmaccuauh yetiuh intlahuiz ipampa ca yaotitlan in quizaya in cana miquia in cana tlamaia
 auh in ompa calaquia xicalanco in quitquia itlatqui ahuitzontzinzan ye no ye in ixquich omitoin tlahtocatilmahtli in tlahtocamaxtli in tlazocueyitl in tlamachio azo tehtenezcayo anozo chicocueyitl ihuan tlahmachuipilli
 auh in iz catqui in imixcoyan itlatqui catca pochteca tepeyo teocuitlatl iuhquin tlahtocayotl conmaquia in ompa tlahtoque

 auh in zam macehualtin intech monequia itznacochtli tepoznacochtli ihuan itztlaehualli neximaloni ihuan huitzauhqui ihuan coyolli ihuan huitzmallotl nocheztli tlalxocotl tochimitl tlacopahtli xochipahtli
 auh in yehuantin teyacanque pochtecatlahtoque tealtianime tecohuanime intiamic catca tlatlahcotli azo cihuatl anozo oquichpiltontli in ompa quimonnamacaya
 auh quin huicaya intlahuiz quin onaquiaya in ahzo cihuatl conaquiaya in tlahuiztli ipampa ca yaotitlan in quizaya in quimimacacia toyaohuan tecuantepecatl tzapotecatl chiauhpanecatl in intzalan quiyaza
 auh in ye on ahcitiuhui yaonepantla achtopa on tlatitlani on tlaihua on tlanonotza on teitohua
 auh in ic nehnemi amo cem ilhuitl in ohtlatoca zan yohualtica
 auh in oahcito titlantin niman huallihua in anahuacatlahtoque in ic quihualnamiquia no hual moyauhchichiuhtihui inchimal inmaccuauh in intlahuiz yetihuitz in ic oncan qui hual namiquia yaonepantla in ic huel on acia in ompa anahuac xicalanco
 auh in o ahcique pochteca in anahuac xicalanco in yehuantin ompa tlahtoque in quipachohua altepetl anahuac niman ye ic quimmaca in ixquich onmococouh in tlahzotilmatli in tlazocueyitl in tlazohuipilli in iaxca ahuitzotzin in ic quimontlapalohua

 ye ihui in in ic teocnenemia in ic quihueyilique in altepetl in mexicayotl ipampa ca nohuian tzaocticatca in anahuacatlalli
 auh ipampa in cenca quintlazotlaya in ahuitzotzin huel iuhquinmah no ipilhuan quinchihuaya

in temazcalli
ihcuac mocalquetza in temazcalli quichihuiliah icuayolicpac zan ica tezontli ihuan motzicoa in tetzontemeh ica zoquitl in temazcalli ahmo huel huehyi mochihua zan onaqui nahui ahnozo chicuacen tlacah
achtotipa quitlaliliayah in ixic ica campa quizaz in poctli inon itlatlacoyocton quichihuiliayah inacacic axcan zan mocoyonia ica campa quizaz in tzoatl no quichihuiliah in itlexic nican tlepitzalo ica mototoniz in temazcalli ihuan motlecuiltia in tlecuahuitl ica ocototon
ihcuac ye oquitlanqueh ye oquichiuhqueh in temazcalli motemoah in teoyoticatahtli ihuan monotza in teopixqui
ipan tonalli ihcuac moteochihuaz no motocayotia ahci in teopixqui temazcalco quiteochihua ica popochtli ihuan quitocayotia ica in quixtianotocaitl quemen jose xuan luis ihuan occequintin yece in teoyoticatahtli achto quitlamahuichihchihuah in temazcalli ica xochitl chinaamatl quilacatzoa ica xochicuzcatl ihuan quimahmana in xochitl icehcecac ica campa calacoah no itech monequi in teoyoticathatli quitemacaz quitetlacuiliz galletahtoton necuhtli pahchichic ihuan tlacueponiz
in ahquin iaxca in temazcalli quitemaca tlacualli alozmolli ayohhuachmolli yemolli quemmanian tlemolli ica yetamalli ahnozo ahuaxtamalli quemmanian no motemaca in tepachnecuhtli
ihcuac aca motemaz tlepitzalo ihtic in tlexictli intla monequi huel totonqui yez in temazcalli motlalilia in ahuacuahuitl ahnozo tamazquicuahuitl intla ahmo monequi cenca totonqui zan motlalilia ococuahuitl ihcuac ye netemaloz achto mototonia in atl ihtic in temazcalli itech in itlexic intla ye tlacuauhtotonqui motzacua in tlexictli ica centetl tepatlachtli inin motzicoa ica zoquitl ihuan mixtilinaltia ica tetoton
aquihuan mopacazqueh quinechicoah in tecapolxihuitl ahnozo capolxihuitl mochinin cenca yamanqui ica mototonia in tonacayo icanin xihuitl nexiuhhuilo quemanian nexiuhhuilo ica ahhuiyayalizxihuitl itoca teyahuitl poleoxihuitl
ihcuac ye ototonix in temazcalli ihtic aca calaqui quiquixtia in tlecohcotoccuahuitl tlen oc popoca ihuan quitlaxilia in atzintli ipan tlexihcotezontli ica tleconexquizaz

noihqui panohuayan tlachpanahtica

mantlacualli huicci manmotlaxcalmana manmochihua pantzin ihuan tetexhuelic
estufa electricah estufa gasolinah ihuan chapopotl ihuan cente tepoztlahuic citini tiquintequitilia inic huicciz pantzin ihuan tetexhuelic

ihuan nohuan
ompa nochan momochco malacateticpac tlaca tequiti ihuan cihuame tlaxcaloa tlacualchihua oncuan on yecoz tlacatl ye mayana nochi tlacuali za tequichia ihqui in ica nemia nochantlaca
noca yahue tlaca tequitizque cihuame noihqui tlacoa ompa tianquizco campa monamaca nacatl yetl tlaoli nochi tlen monequiz cuahuitl tecoli xochicuali nochi in itech monequi cihuame ipan calli yomocuepque cihuame tianquiztli quitlipantlalia tlacuali ihuan huici quizaca atzintli ica ce ticaxalotin nozo tepozcaxtin ihuan tla yohuala tenamic tzicuini cihuatontli quicoaz neuhtli
iqui in temachtiani niauh nimitztlanonotzaz inin tlatoli itech naltepeuh ihuan nonemiliz
momochco malacateticpac naltepeuh itocan milpa alta caxtilancopa nozo asuncion milpa alta ihuan intzalan tetepeme cuauhtzin ihuan teuhtli
nota nonan cuali otlatoaya macehualcopa ihuan caxtilancopa
achtopa inin tlatoli itech notatzin niauh nitlanonotzaz ihcuac nehua nitepiton notatzin ayemo huel omotequitiliaya zan yehuatl omotlaquichiliaya cuentla mahtlactli huan ome metoton huan omotlachiquiliaya oncuan on mochihuaz neuhtli ican ayemo miac tepilhuan oyeya cuali opanoaloya ica neuhtomin ipan on tonaltin ipatiuh ce litro neuhtli yeyi centavo ica ipan tica on amo omopiaya litros que axan ica tlatamachihualo iman tica on oyeya almontin tlacualmon ihuan cuarteron
